      <p>
       This is a
       <b>
        list of solar eclipses in the 9th century BC
       </b>
       . During the period 900 to 801 BC there were 225
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse" title="Solar eclipse">
        solar eclipses
       </a>
       of which 80 were partial, 75 were annular (two
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse#Terminology" title="Solar eclipse">
        non-central
       </a>
       ), 66 were total (two non-central), and 4 were hybrids. The greatest number of eclipses in one year was four, in 884 BC and 866 BC.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nasa_catalog_list_1-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-nasa_catalog_list-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <div style="clear:both;">
      </div>
